````text
============================================================

=== Comment [3179375515] ===
Type: CODE | By: AvanishKulkarni | Status: ○ no reply
File: harmony-frontend/src/components/message/ThreadView.tsx:13
URL: https://github.com/CS485-Harmony/Harmony/pull/614#discussion_r3179375515

--- Code Context ---
@@ -13,6 +13,7 @@ import { formatMessageTimestamp } from '@/lib/utils';
 import { getThreadMessagesAction } from '@/app/actions/getThreadMessages';
--- End Code Context ---

**Minor: `handleReplySent` raw-appends without dedup, creating a potential duplicate in the rare SSE-first race.**

`handleReplySent` does `setReplies(prev => [...prev, reply])`. With `incomingReply` now wired, the same reply can arrive via two paths when the SSE fires before `createReplyAction` resolves:

1. SSE → `incomingReply` → `appendUniqueReplies` appends reply
2. `createReplyAction` resolves → `handleReplySent` → raw append → duplicate

`appendUniqueReplies` already handles this. Consider:

```ts
const handleReplySent = useCallback((reply: Message) => {
  setReplies(prev => appendUniqueReplies(prev, [reply]));
  setIsComposerOpen(false);
}, []);
```

Not blocking since the race is rare in practice, but it is the same family of issue as the one just fixed.

============================================================

=== Comment [4217370939] ===
Type: REVIEW | By: AvanishKulkarni | Status: ○ no reply
URL: https://github.com/CS485-Harmony/Harmony/pull/614#pullrequestreview-4217370939

## PR Review Guidelines Checklist

- [x] **1. Prioritize Logic over Style** — Logic is clean; utility functions are well-factored. One logic correctness issue found (see below).
- [x] **2. Security First** — No new surface area; utilities are pure functions with no I/O.
- [x] **3. Architectural Alignment** — Follows existing patterns (render-phase derived state, SSE handler delegation).
- [x] **4. Issue Completion** — All six acceptance criteria for #503 are satisfied: reply UI exists, `createReply`/`getThreadMessages` are wired, thread list updates, pagination dedup is correct, required fields are present.
- [ ] **5. No Nitpicking / 6. Avoid Repetition / 7. Iterative Reviews** — The three previous concerns (non-null assertion, derived-state comment, move `appendUniqueReplies`) were all addressed in commit `90490f8d`. One new correctness issue found that was not raised before.
- [x] **8. Prevent CI Failures** — No syntax errors, missing imports, or obvious test breakage.

---

## Review

The overall approach is sound — centralising dedup logic in `message-threading.ts` and sharing a single `trackCreatedMessage` path for both the composer and SSE is the right design. The previous concerns have been resolved. One new correctness bug is present.

### `harmony-frontend/src/components/message/ThreadView.tsx` – double-count race when SSE beats the tRPC response

`ThreadView.handleReplyCreated` (line 240) still calls `onReplyCountChange?.(1)`, which adds 1 to `localReplyCount` in `MessageItem`. At the same time, `trackCreatedMessage` in `HarmonyShell` now bumps the parent`s `replyCount` in `localMessages` via `mergeCreatedMessageIntoChannelMessages`, so the `prevReplyCount` sync in `MessageItem` will eventually set `localReplyCount` to the authoritative value.

This works correctly only when the tRPC HTTP response arrives *before* the SSE event. The race goes wrong in the other order:

```
1. Backend creates reply → emits Redis pub/sub event
2. SSE arrives: message.replyCount becomes 1
3. MessageItem re-renders: prevReplyCount(0) ≠ 1 → sync sets localReplyCount = 1
4. createReplyAction() resolves → onReplyCountChange(1) → localReplyCount = 2  ← WRONG
5. message.replyCount stays 1, prevReplyCount is already 1 → no further sync
```

The SSE-first path is realistic: Redis pub/sub on the same backend instance often delivers before the HTTP round-trip completes.

**Fix:** Remove the `onReplyCountChange?.(1)` call from `ThreadView.handleReplyCreated`. The parent count is now managed authoritatively through `mergeCreatedMessageIntoChannelMessages` triggered by both the SSE path and the `handleMessageSent` path. The `onReplyCountChange` prop itself can stay for other callers, but `ThreadView` should no longer push a delta that races with the centralised count update.

============================================================

=== Comment [4216798758] ===
Type: REVIEW | By: AvanishKulkarni | Status: ○ no reply
URL: https://github.com/CS485-Harmony/Harmony/pull/614#pullrequestreview-4216798758

## Overview

This PR correctly fixes the threading state update bugs from #503: reply counts now increment exactly once whether the reply comes from the composer or SSE, `ThreadView` merges incoming replies without duplicates, and `localReplyCount` in `MessageItem` stays in sync with the underlying prop. The implementation is focused and minimal — good scope discipline.

A few targeted suggestions below.

### Double-count interaction (non-obvious but not a bug)

When the thread composer sends a reply, `ThreadView.handleReplyCreated` fires `onReplyCountChange(1)` which bumps `localReplyCount` by delta. Shortly after, `trackCreatedMessage` → `mergeCreatedMessageIntoChannelMessages` updates `message.replyCount` on the prop. The render-phase `prevReplyCount` sync then **replaces** `localReplyCount` with the prop value, so the delta increment is effectively overwritten. Net result is correct, but the two-path handoff is fragile — a short comment would prevent a future contributor from removing one path thinking the other makes it redundant.

### `appendUniqueReplies` placement

The function is a pure dedup utility on `Message[]`, parallel in role to `mergeCreatedMessageIntoChannelMessages`. Both belong in `lib/message-threading.ts` where they can be co-tested. Leaving it private to `ThreadView.tsx` means it is currently untested in isolation.

### Tests

The three new test cases cover the main scenarios well. Gaps worth noting:
- No test for the `onReplyCountChange` + render-phase sync interaction.
- `appendUniqueReplies` is untested in isolation; moving it to the shared lib would fix this automatically.
````

That is a real issue in the same race family, so I’m fixing it and will reply to the new review/comment after another commit.
